<br><font size="+2"><b><a name="ibachasàaka"></a>ibachasàaka</b> </font>
<font size="+2">to gain (weight); to have extended in some respect, have gained, have added on</font>
&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">CHA-</font>
&nbsp; [/ibachasàa-ka<sup>1</sup>]
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chibachasàakasakáamo, chibaybaayok.
 <i>You've gained some weight it seems.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Chabaybaayok amibachássàakaasiiso, oompalifíhtonkan.
 <i>My weight has extended so I guess I ate too much.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Máakaya chabachasàakaamoolo toknaawa táɬɬìipaspókkòoliyok annàahotoha.
 <i>I'm really extended now that I have a thousand dollars.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Píila yaabannit sòolit ihto mintóot ibachasàakaimon holihtachòoba yiɬápliimok ìisaamon holihta háhpa stoɬàachit yaabannit oshopaapíɬkat istamaakahchoolikha.
 <i>They would just carry it on their shoulder and carry it in the crook of their arms and if another field was to be added on to, then some would be there to tear down the old fence and some would be bringing the new fence rails on their shoulder and would go and stack them up.</i> <font size="0">(NWK)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>Usage: </i>For some speakers, this is used of third person only; others accept with second persons as well, first person acceptable but not preferred form.

 <i>It's his/hers/its.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>They wanted them to belong to the Indians.</i> <font size="0">(NIA)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Ohibisno.
 <i>It's theirs.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Yok chibisnòoli?
 <i>Is this yours?</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Ifaya Koora ibisnooliimon sobàylilo.
 <i>I know that dog belongs to Cora.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Amanɬiyafóot máalifon aⁿhínnàataamók ibisno holchifak òmmin.
 <i>He leads me in the paths of righteousness for his name's sake.</i> <font size="0">(TTP)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>

&nbsp;<font color="#800080" size="+1">-LI/CHA-</font>
&nbsp;(<i>ihannichitiska, ihannichitilka, ihannichitaska</i>)
&nbsp;(<i>ihannichiska, ihannichilka, ihannichaska</i>)

 <i>Var: iyannichi</i>
 <i>Var: ihannochi</i>

 <i>Lower it a bit.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

 <i>You lower me down.</i><font face="Arial">»</font>

&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Máamòosin akkat oɬaamon akkat àayat akkamíhchit imakanochiik oolakanoochiimon yon tayyiha tòklohchon ohiⁿfaylilaak onkatóon ommin.
 <i>And he did all of that that way because he was improving things and if he brought peace then what they had promised him was these two women.</i> <font size="0">(HCW)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Holihta imakanóochikáhmiya oittimapíilaastóobahchoolikha.
 <i>When they rebuilt a fence they continued to help each other.</i> <font size="0">(NWK)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
&nbsp;<font face="Arial">«</font>Tanahlok amaakatok Chahtahaakok nàasooton imakanoochiikat stíisafòokon híichatáskat `amahilkaskìi' homankok.
 <i>They got out (of the boat) and went over there and they noticed that the Choctaws seemed to be preparing for something so they said `Let's go!'</i> <font size="0">(HCW)</font><font face="Arial">»</font>
